## Provider
**SiliconFlow** (`https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1`, OpenAI-compatible chat completions).

## Grammar capability
- **Documented support:** JSON-mode structured output via `response_format={"type":"json_object"}`.
- **Also documented:** `tools[].function.strict` for **function-calling argument schema adherence** (subset of JSON Schema).
- **Not documented (in official docs I checked):** explicit grammar-constrained decoding via **CFG/BNF/EBNF/regex** for assistant text generation.

## Request shape
- Chat completions request includes:
  - `stream: boolean`
  - `response_format: { type: string }` (guide shows `type: "json_object"`)
  - `tools: [...]` with function definitions
  - `tools[].function.parameters` (JSON Schema-like)
  - `tools[].function.strict: boolean` (strict schema adherence for function call args)

## Grammar dialect and caveats
- **Dialect actually documented for constrained behavior:** JSON object mode (`response_format.type="json_object"`), plus function-arg schema constraints using a **subset of JSON Schema** when `strict=true`.
- **Caveats documented:**
  - Handle incomplete JSON edge cases.
  - Set `max_tokens` carefully to avoid truncated JSON.
  - `strict` note is tied to function-calling parameters, not general free-text CFG/regex decoding.
- **Inference:** No official SiliconFlow doc page found describing regex/CFG grammar decoding fields (as of **2026-02-14**).

## Streaming fields
When `stream=true`:
- Transport: SSE, terminates with `data: [DONE]`.
- Chunk object type: `object: "chat.completion.chunk"`.
- Relevant fields in chunks/examples:
  - `choices[].delta.role`
  - `choices[].delta.content`
  - `choices[].delta.reasoning_content`
  - `choices[].finish_reason`
  - top-level `id`, `created`, `model` (and `usage` appears in examples).
- No dedicated streaming field for grammar/constraint state is documented.

## Sources (URLs)
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/api-reference/chat-completions/chat-completions  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/api-reference/chat-completions/chat-completions.md  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/userguide/guides/json-mode  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/userguide/guides/json-mode.md  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/llms.txt  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/llms-full.txt

def function_call_playground(prompt):
    messages = [{'role': 'user', 'content': prompt}]

        model="deepseek-ai/DeepSeek-V2.5",

        top_p=0.95,
        stream=False,
        tools=tools
    )

    # Â§ÑÁêÜ API ËøîÂõûÁöÑÂ∑•ÂÖ∑Ë∞ÉÁî®ËØ∑Ê±Ç

    func1_args = response.choices[0].message.tool_calls[0].function.arguments
    func1_out = eval(f'{func1_name}(**{func1_args})')

> ## Documentation Index
> Fetch the complete documentation index at: https://docs.siliconflow.cn/llms.txt
> Use this file to discover all available pages before exploring further.

# JSON schema

## 1. Use Cases

Currently, the SiliconFlow large model API platform defaults to generating unstructured text. However, in certain use cases, you may want the model to output content in a structured format. However, instructing the large model directly with prompts may not yield the correct structured output.

As a standardized and lightweight data exchange format, the JSON schema is an important feature that supports the large model API to produce structured outputs. When you call the large model's API to make a request, the model returns results in JSON format, which is easy for humans to read and write, and also easy for machines to parse and generate.

Now, all major language models on the SiliconFlow platform, except for the R1 series and V3 models from DeepSeek, support JSON mode, allowing the model to output JSON-formatted strings to ensure that the model outputs in the expected structure, making it easier to logically parse the output content.

For example, you can now try structured output using the SiliconFlow API for the following cases:

* Building a news database from company-related reports, including news titles and links.
* Extracting sentiment analysis structures from product purchase reviews, including sentiment polarity (positive, negative, neutral), sentiment intensity, and sentiment keywords.
* Extracting product lists from purchase history, including product information, recommendation reasons, prices, and promotional information.

thinking
**Composing concise documentation summary**
codex
## Provider
**SiliconFlow** (`https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1`, OpenAI-compatible chat completions).

## Grammar capability
- **Documented support:** JSON-mode structured output via `response_format={"type":"json_object"}`.
- **Also documented:** `tools[].function.strict` for **function-calling argument schema adherence** (subset of JSON Schema).
- **Not documented (in official docs I checked):** explicit grammar-constrained decoding via **CFG/BNF/EBNF/regex** for assistant text generation.

## Request shape
- Chat completions request includes:
  - `stream: boolean`
  - `response_format: { type: string }` (guide shows `type: "json_object"`)
  - `tools: [...]` with function definitions
  - `tools[].function.parameters` (JSON Schema-like)
  - `tools[].function.strict: boolean` (strict schema adherence for function call args)

## Grammar dialect and caveats
- **Dialect actually documented for constrained behavior:** JSON object mode (`response_format.type="json_object"`), plus function-arg schema constraints using a **subset of JSON Schema** when `strict=true`.
- **Caveats documented:**
  - Handle incomplete JSON edge cases.
  - Set `max_tokens` carefully to avoid truncated JSON.
  - `strict` note is tied to function-calling parameters, not general free-text CFG/regex decoding.
- **Inference:** No official SiliconFlow doc page found describing regex/CFG grammar decoding fields (as of **2026-02-14**).

## Streaming fields
When `stream=true`:
- Transport: SSE, terminates with `data: [DONE]`.
- Chunk object type: `object: "chat.completion.chunk"`.
- Relevant fields in chunks/examples:
  - `choices[].delta.role`
  - `choices[].delta.content`
  - `choices[].delta.reasoning_content`
  - `choices[].finish_reason`
  - top-level `id`, `created`, `model` (and `usage` appears in examples).
- No dedicated streaming field for grammar/constraint state is documented.

## Sources (URLs)
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/api-reference/chat-completions/chat-completions  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/api-reference/chat-completions/chat-completions.md  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/userguide/guides/json-mode  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/en/userguide/guides/json-mode.md  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/llms.txt  
- https://docs.siliconflow.cn/llms-full.txt
